// The Replacements
actor SamsaraSlotTwo_ROTWB replaces ShotgunNew
{
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0 NoDelay ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("Samsara_SpawnSlot",3,1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("Samsara_SpawnSlot",2,1)
			stop
	}
}

// The Monsters
ACTOR ShotgunCat_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterBeastMediumTotalGib replaces ShotgunCat
{
	Game Doom
	Health 15
    Damage 1
	Radius 20
	Height 40
	Mass 20
    Speed 10
    Scale 0.8
	PainChance 170
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
    +LOOKALLAROUND
    +DONTGIB
    +NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
    SeeSound "CATSIGHT"
	AttackSound "shotguy/attack"
	PainSound "CATPAIN"
	DeathSound "CATDIE"
    DropItem "SamsaraAmmo1Small_ROTWB", 125, 5
	Tag "Shotgun Cat"
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	Obituary "You were perforated by the bullets of the shotgun cat!"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		SPOS A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		SPOS BB 3 A_Chase
        SPOS BB 0 A_PlaySound("PASPLAN3")
        SPOS DD 3 A_Chase
        SPOS DD 0 A_PlaySound("PASPLAN4")
        SPOS CC 3 A_Chase
        SPOS CC 0 A_PlaySound("PASPLAN3")
        SPOS DD 3 A_Chase
        SPOS DD 0 A_PlaySound("PASPLAN4")
		Loop
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		SPOS E 10 A_FaceTarget
		SPOS F 10 A_CustomBulletAttack(5, 0, 1, 3, "BulletPuff")
		SPOS E 10
		Goto See
	Pain:
		SPOS G 2 A_Pain
		SPOS G 2
		Goto See
	Pain.MightyBoot:
        TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
        SPOS G 2 A_FaceTarget
        TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
        SPOS G 16 A_Pain
        Goto See
	Death:
 		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		SPOS I 4 A_Scream
		SPOS J 4 A_NoBlocking
        SPOS K 4
		SPOS L 4
        SPOS M 4
		SPOS H -1
		Stop
	Death.PainkillerStake:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Painkiller_MonsterKill")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Painkiller_IsItGibbed")==1,"PainkillerGib")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Painkiller_RunStake",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	StakeDeath:
		SPOS G 2
		Loop
    Raise:
        SPOS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyZorched",1,"ZorchRaise")
		SPOS H 1
        SPOS M 4
        SPOS L 4
        SPOS K 4
        SPOS J 4
        SPOS I 4
        Goto See
	ZorchRaise:
		"####" "#" 1 A_UnsetShootable
		"####" "#" 1 A_SpawnItem("SpawnFire2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("archvile/resummon")
		"####" "#" 1 A_TakeInventory("EnemyZorched",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.2,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.3,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.4,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.5,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.6,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.8,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(1,0)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetShootable
		Goto See
    Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		SPOS G 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		SPOS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		SPOS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
    }
}

actor ShotgunCat_Samsara_Shrink : ShotgunCat_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			SPOS G 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			SPOS AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

ACTOR DemonCat_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterBeastLargeTotalGib replaces DemonCat
{
	Health 150
	PainChance 180
	Speed 18
	Radius 20
	Height 60
    Scale 0.7
	Mass 40
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP +FASTER +FASTMELEE
    +LOOKALLAROUND
    +DONTGIB
    +NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
    SeeSound "RAWR"
	AttackSound "SWOOSH"
	DeathSound "GROUND"
    PainSound "RAWR2"
	Tag "Berserker Kitty"
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	Obituary "You were killed by a berserker kitty!"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		SARG A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		SARG AA 3 A_Chase
        SARG BB 3 A_Chase
        SARG A 0 A_PlaySound("STAMPF1")
        SARG AA 3 A_Chase
        SARG CC 3 A_Chase
        SARG A 0 A_PlaySound("STAMPF2")
        Loop
	Melee:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
        SARG H 2 A_FaceTarget
        SARG H 2 A_PlaySound("SWOOSH")
        SARG I 3 A_SkelFist
        SARG J 3 A_FaceTarget
        SARG H 7 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
	Pain:
		SARG F 4 A_Pain
		Goto See
    Pain.MightyBoot:
        TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
        SARG F 2 A_FaceTarget
        TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(12)
        SARG F 16 A_Pain
        Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		SARG F 5
		SARG H 3
        SARG K 3
        SARG G 0 A_NoBlocking
        SARG G 0 A_Scream
        SARG G 5 Radius_Quake(1,10,0,10,0)
		SARG G -1
		Stop
	Death.PainkillerStake:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Painkiller_MonsterKill")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Painkiller_IsItGibbed")==1,"PainkillerGib")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Painkiller_RunStake",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	StakeDeath:
		SARG F 2
		Loop
	Raise:
		SARG A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyZorched",1,"ZorchRaise")
		SARG K 4
		SARG H 4
		SARG F 4
		Goto See
	ZorchRaise:
		"####" "#" 1 A_UnsetShootable
		"####" "#" 1 A_SpawnItem("SpawnFire2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("archvile/resummon")
		"####" "#" 1 A_TakeInventory("EnemyZorched",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.2,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.3,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.4,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.5,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.6,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.8,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(1,0)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetShootable
		Goto See
	Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		SARG F 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		SARG A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		SARG A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}
}

actor DemonCat_Samsara_Shrink : DemonCat_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL

	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 8
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			SARG F 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			SARG AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG A 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG A 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG B 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG C 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			stop

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)

			Goto Squish

actor ChaingunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect : ChaingunCat_Samsara

actor WizardCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect : WizardCat_Samsara

		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		LEGS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop	
	}

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

ACTOR WizardCatBlack_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterBeastMediumTotalGib replaces WizardCatBlack
{
	Health 150
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 20
    Scale 0.8
	Speed 12
	PainChance 200
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
    +LOOKALLAROUND
    +DONTGIB
    +NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
	SeeSound "WIZB1"
	PainSound "WIZB2"
	DeathSound "WIZB3"
	HitObituary "$OB_IMPHIT"
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	Tag "Wizard Cat"
	Obituary "You were burned by the wizard cat!"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		VOOD AABBCCBB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		VOOD AAAABBBBCCCCBBBB 2 A_VileChase
		Loop
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		VOOD D 6 A_FaceTarget
		VOOD E 3 A_TroopAttack
        VOOD E 3 A_TroopAttack
        VOOD E 3 A_TroopAttack
        VOOD D 3
		Goto See
    Heal:
        VOOD D 5
        VOOD D 5
        Goto See
	Pain:
		VOOD F 2 A_Pain
		VOOD F 2
		Goto See
    Pain.MightyBoot:
        TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
        VOOD F 2 A_FaceTarget
        TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(12)
        VOOD F 16 A_Pain
        Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		VOOD F 5 A_Scream
		VOOD G 4
		VOOD H 3 A_NoBlocking
		VOOD I -1
		Stop
	Death.PainkillerStake:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Painkiller_MonsterKill")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Painkiller_IsItGibbed")==1,"PainkillerGib")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Painkiller_RunStake",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	StakeDeath:
		VOOD F 2
		Loop
    Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		VOOD F 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WizardCatBlack_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WizardCatBlack_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WizardCatBlack_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WizardCatBlack_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WizardCatBlack_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WizardCatBlack_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WizardCatBlack_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WizardCatBlack_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		VOOD A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		VOOD A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop	
	}
}

actor WizardCatBlack_Samsara_Shrink : WizardCatBlack_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 8
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			VOOD F 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			VOOD AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			VOOD A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			VOOD A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			VOOD B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			VOOD B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			VOOD C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			VOOD C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			VOOD D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			VOOD D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("MasterDeadToken", 1, AAPTR_Master)
			TNT1 A 0
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}

ACTOR ShotgunCatFloat_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterMechanicalMediumTotalGib replaces ShotgunCatFloat
{
	Game Doom
	Health 15
    Damage 1
	Radius 20
	Height 128
	Mass 20
    Speed 16
    Scale 0.8
	PainChance 0
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
    +LOOKALLAROUND
    +DONTGIB
    +NOGRAVITY
    +FLOATBOB
    +NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
    SeeSound "CATSIGHT"
	AttackSound "shotguy/attack"
	PainSound "CATPAIN"
	DeathSound "CATDIE"
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	Tag "Floating Shotgun Cat"
	Obituary "You were perforated by the bullets of the shotgun cat!"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0 NoDelay A_GiveInventory("IsAFlyingActor")
	Spawn2:
		FLOA AAAABBBB 3 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		FLOA AAAABBBB 3 A_Chase  
		Loop
	Missile:
		FLOA C 10 A_FaceTarget
		FLOA D 10 A_CustomBulletAttack( 5, 0, 1, 3, "BulletPuff")
		FLOA C 10
		Goto See
	Pain:
		FLOA A 0
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
 		FLOA E 4 A_Scream
        FLOA L 4 A_NoBlocking
        FLOA K 4
        FLOA J 4
        FLOA I 4
        FLOA L 4
        FLOA K 4
        FLOA J 4
        FLOA I 4
        FLOA L 5
        FLOA K 5
        FLOA J 6
        FLOA I 7
        FLOA G -1 
        Stop
	Death.PainkillerStake:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Painkiller_MonsterKill")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Painkiller_IsItGibbed")==1,"PainkillerGib")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Painkiller_RunStake",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	StakeDeath:
		FLOA E 2
		Loop
	Raise:
	    FLOA A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyZorched",1,"ZorchRaise")
        SPOS H 1
        SPOS M 4
        SPOS L 4
        SPOS K 4
        SPOS J 4
        SPOS I 4
        Goto See
	ZorchRaise:
		"####" "#" 1 A_UnsetShootable
		"####" "#" 1 A_SpawnItem("SpawnFire2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("archvile/resummon")
		"####" "#" 1 A_TakeInventory("EnemyZorched",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.2,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.3,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.4,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.5,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.6,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.8,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(1,0)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetShootable
		Goto See
    Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		FLOA A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCatFloat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCatFloat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCatFloat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCatFloat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCatFloat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCatFloat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCatFloat_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		FLOA A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		FLOA A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop	
    }
}

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0

			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("MasterDeadToken", 1, AAPTR_Master)
			TNT1 A 0
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("MasterDeadToken", 1, AAPTR_Master)
			TNT1 A 0
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}

actor KamikaziGuy_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterMechanicalMediumTotalGib replaces KamikaziGuy
{
	obituary "You were mowed down by a flying saucer cat!"
	health 20
	radius 16
	height 56
	mass 100
	Scale 0.7
	speed 12
	MONSTER
	+LOOKALLAROUND
	+FLOORCLIP
	+DONTGIB
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+NOVERTICALMELEERANGE
    +NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	Tag "Flying Saucer Cat"
	SeeSound "UFOSEE"
	states
	{
	Spawn:
		BKAM A 0 A_StopSoundEx ("soundslot5")
		BKAM AB 5 A_LookEx (0, 0, 0, 1024) 
		loop
	Idle:
		BKAM A 0 A_StopSoundEx ("soundslot5")
		BKAM A 10 A_LookEx (0, 0, 0, 1024) 
		BKAM A 0 A_Jump (8, "IdleNoise")
		loop
	IdleNoise:
		BKAM A 0
		goto Idle
	See:
		BKAM A 0 A_PlaySoundEx ("kamikazi/scream", "soundslot5", 1)
		BKAM A 2 A_FaceTarget
		BKAM A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(56, "Melee", 0)
		BKAM A 2 A_Recoil (-5)
		BKAM A 2 A_FaceTarget
		BKAM B 0 A_JumpIfCloser(56, "Melee", 0)
		BKAM B 2 A_Recoil (-5)
		BKAM B 2 A_FaceTarget
		BKAM B 0 A_JumpIfCloser(56, "Melee", 0)
		BKAM B 2 A_Recoil (-5)
		BKAM A 2 A_FaceTarget
		BKAM A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(56, "Melee", 0)
		BKAM A 2 A_Recoil (-5)
	CheckSee:
		BKAM A 0 A_CheckSight ("Navigate")
		goto See
	Navigate:
		BKAM AABBAABBAABBAABBAABBAABB 2 A_Chase
		goto CheckSee
	Melee:
		BKAM A 0 A_Die
		stop
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		BMBE M 0 bright A_SpawnItem ("KamikaziDamage", 0, 40)
		BMBE M 0 bright A_SpawnItem ("SaucerCatExplosion", 0, 0)
		BMBE M 0 bright A_Stop
		BMBE M 0 bright A_StopSoundEx ("soundslot5")
		BKAM C 5 bright A_PlaySound ("weapons/rocklx")
		BKAM D 5 bright
		BKAM E 0 A_PlaySound ("PUPPETHIT")
		BKAM E 5 A_NoBlocking
		BKAM F -1
		stop
    Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		BKAM A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("KamikaziGuy_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("KamikaziGuy_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("KamikaziGuy_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("KamikaziGuy_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("KamikaziGuy_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("KamikaziGuy_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("KamikaziGuy_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("KamikaziGuy_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		BKAM A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		BKAM A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop	
	}

			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("MasterDeadToken", 1, AAPTR_Master)
			TNT1 A 0
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

ACTOR FlyingKitty_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterMechanicalMediumTotalGib replaces FlyingKitty
{
	Game Doom
	Health 300
    Scale 0.8
	Radius 25
	Height 56
	Mass 9999999
	Speed 20
	PainChance 100
	Monster
    +MISSILEMORE
	+NOGRAVITY
	+FLOORCLIP
    +LOOKALLAROUND
    +DONTGIB
    +FLOATBOB
    +NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
	SeeSound "COPTER1"
    PainSound "COPTERPAIN"
	DeathSound "COPTDIE2"
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	Tag "Copter Kitty"
	Obituary "You were killed by the copter kitty!"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0 NoDelay A_GiveInventory("IsAFlyingActor")
	Spawn2:
		COPT AABBAACC 4 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		COPT A 4 A_Chase
        COPT A 0 A_PlaySound("HELICO4")
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
		COPT A 4 A_Chase
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
		COPT B 4 A_Chase
        COPT A 0 A_PlaySound("HELICO4")
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
		COPT B 4 A_Chase
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
		COPT A 4 A_Chase
        COPT A 0 A_PlaySound("HELICO4")
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
		COPT A 4 A_Chase
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
		COPT C 4 A_Chase
        COPT A 0 A_PlaySound("HELICO4")
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
		COPT C 4 A_Chase
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
		Loop
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		COPT E 1 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
		COPT E 4 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
		COPT F 10 A_CustomMissile("OfficerCatCannon", 32, 14)
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
		COPT E 5 A_FaceTarget
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
        COPT F 10 A_CustomMissile("OfficerCatCannon", 32, 14)
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
        COPT E 5 A_FaceTarget
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
        COPT F 10 A_CustomMissile("OfficerCatCannon", 32, 14)
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
        COPT E 5 A_FaceTarget
        COPT A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(250, "DropBomb", 1)
		Goto See
	Pain:
        COPT D 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOATBOB", FALSE)
		COPT D 3 A_Pain
		COPT A 2
		COPT D 3
		COPT A 2
        COPT D 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOATBOB", TRUE)
		Goto See
    Pain.MightyBoot:
        COPT D 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOATBOB", FALSE)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
        COPT D 2 A_FaceTarget
        TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
        COPT D 16 A_Pain
		COPT D 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOATBOB", TRUE)
        goto See
    DropBomb:
        COPT N 5
        COPT N 0 A_SpawnItem("DropBarrel_Samsara", 0, 0)
        COPT M 20
        COPT M 1
        Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		COPT D 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOATBOB", FALSE)
        COPT D 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOCLIP", TRUE)
        COPT D 0 A_NoBlocking
		COPT D 3 A_Scream
        COPT D 0
		COPT GJIHGJIHGJIHGJIHGJIHGJIHGJIHGJIHGJIHGJIHGJIHGJIHGJIHGJIHGJIHGJIHGJIH 4 A_CheckFloor("Death2")
		Loop
    Death2:
        COPT L 0 A_SpawnItem("BoomBarrelCorpse_Samsara", 0, 0)
        COPT L 0
        COPT L 2
        COPT K 0 Radius_Quake(2,10,0,10,0)
        COPT K -1
        Stop
    Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		COPT D 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FlyingKitty_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FlyingKitty_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FlyingKitty_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FlyingKitty_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FlyingKitty_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FlyingKitty_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FlyingKitty_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FlyingKitty_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		COPT A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		COPT A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop	
	}
}

actor FlyingKitty_Samsara_Shrink : FlyingKitty_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	-COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			COPT A 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			COPT AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			COPT A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			COPT A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			COPT A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			COPT A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			COPT B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			COPT B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			COPT B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			COPT B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FlyingKitty_Samsara", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)

			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("MasterDeadToken", 1, AAPTR_Master)
			TNT1 A 0
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

		Loop
	See:

        PUNG A 0 A_ChangeFlag("SOLID", FALSE)

        PUNG A 2 A_Chase

        PUNG A 2 A_Chase

        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 0 A_SpawnItem("FishPuddle_Samsara", 0, 0)
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 0 A_Pain
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 0 A_SpawnItem("FishPuddle_Samsara", 0, 0)
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 0 A_SpawnItem("FishPuddle_Samsara", 0, 0)
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 2 A_Chase
        PUNG A 0 A_SpawnItem("FishPuddle_Samsara", 0, 0)
        FISH EEEEFFFFEEEE 2 A_Chase
        Loop
	Melee:
		FISH A 0 A_ChangeFlag("SHOOTABLE", TRUE)
        PUNG A 0 A_ChangeFlag("SOLID", TRUE)
        FISH A 0 A_Pain
        FISH A 0 A_FaceTarget
        FISH ABC 3
        FISH D 3 A_SargAttack
        FISH CDCBA 3
		Goto See
	Pain:
		FISH A 0 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		FISH I 1 A_Scream
		FISH IJK 3
        FISH L 3 A_NoBlocking
        FISH MN 3
		Stop
	}

ACTOR PsychoCat_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterBeastMediumTotalGib replaces PsychoCat

	+FLOORCLIP
    +LOOKALLAROUND

		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.5,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.6,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.8,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)

		Goto See

		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))

	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)

    }

actor PsychoCat_Samsara_Shrink : PsychoCat_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 8
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			PSYC A 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			PSYC AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
