			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			PUMB D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			PUMB D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ChaingunCatBigCurl_Samsara", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("MasterDeadToken", 1, AAPTR_Master)
			TNT1 A 0
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}

ACTOR RoboCat_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterRoboticLarge replaces RoboCat
{
	Health 300
	Speed 16
	Radius 32
	Height 64
    Scale 1
	Mass 500
    PainChance 150
    MeleeRange 150
	PainSound "LEGSHIT"
    +NOBLOOD
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP +FASTER +FASTMELEE
    +LOOKALLAROUND
    +DONTGIB
    +NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
    SeeSound "RAWR"
	AttackSound "SWOOSH"
	DeathSound "GROUND"
	Tag "Robot Kitty"
	Obituary "You were killed by a robot kitty!"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		ROBO A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		ROBO BB 4 A_Chase
        ROBO BB 0 A_PlaySound("ROBST1")
        ROBO AD 4 A_Chase
        ROBO CC 4 A_Chase
        ROBO BB 0 A_PlaySound("ROBST2")
        ROBO AD 4 A_Chase
        Loop
    Pain:
        ROBO D 0 A_CustomMissile ("RoboCatCog", 60, 0, random(0,360), 2, 24)
        ROBO I 4 A_Pain
        Goto See
	Pain.MightyBoot:
        TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
        ROBO I 2 A_FaceTarget
        TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
        ROBO I 16 A_Pain
        Goto See
	Melee:
        TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		ROBO D 3 A_FaceTarget
        ROBY A 3 A_Recoil (-10)
        ROBY B 3
        ROBY C 3 A_SkelFist
        ROBY D 3 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
    Death:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(-25, "ActuallyDead")
		ROBO DA 3
        ROBO I 3
        ROBO F 3
		ROBO G 3
        ROBO G 0 Radius_Quake(1,10,0,10,0)
        ROBO G 0 A_NoBlocking
        ROBO H 3
        ROBO E 3 
		ROBO E 100   /////leuchtet mit Augen
        ROBO Y 2 A_PlaySound("INTDO3")
        ROBO E 2
        ROBO Y 2
        ROBO E 2
        ROBO Y 2
        ROBO E 100
        ROBO Y 2 A_PlaySound("INTDO3")
        ROBO E 2
        ROBO Y 2
        ROBO E 2
        ROBO Y 2
        ROBO E 50
        ROBO HEGFIBADA 3
        ROBO F 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Robocat_Samsara",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
        Stop
	ActuallyDead:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		ROBO D 0 A_SpawnItemEx ("SaucerCatExplosion",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
        ROBO G 0 A_NoBlocking
        ROBO D 0 A_Quake(6,15,0,400)
        ROBO D 0 A_CustomMissile ("RoboCatHead_Samsara", 80, 0, random(0,360), 2, 24)
        ROBO D 0 A_CustomMissile ("RoboCatArm_Samsara", 60, 0, random(0,360), 2, 24)
        ROBO D 0 A_CustomMissile ("RoboCatLeg_Samsara", 30, 0, random(0,360), 2, 24)
        ROBO OPN 3
        ROBO N -1
		Stop
	}
}

		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		PPIR A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop	
    }
}

		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		PHAB A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop	
	}
}

actor ShimpawMedium_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterBeastHuge replaces ShimpawMedium
{
	obituary "You were smashed by Meowzeki!"
	health 1900
	radius 32
	height 56
	mass 100
	Scale 1.5

	PainSound "MONSTER2"
	DeathSound "BOINGHI"
	MONSTER
	+LOOKALLAROUND

ACTOR Boss2Schlitten_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterBeastMedium replaces Boss2Schlitten
{
	Game Doom
	SpawnID 20
	Health 300
    Scale 1.5
	Radius 32
	Height 56
	Mass 100
	Speed 8
	PainChance 100
	MeleeThreshold 196
    +MISSILEMORE
    +MISSILEEVENMORE
    +SHOOTABLE
    +NOBLOCKMAP
	+FLOORCLIP
    +NOCLIP
    +THRUACTORS
    +LOOKALLAROUND
    +FLOATBOB
    +NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
	SeeSound "OFFIC2"
    PainSound "PUNCH8"
	DeathSound "CHAINCATDIE"
	MeleeSound "skeleton/melee"
	HitObituary "$OB_UNDEADHIT"
	Obituary "You were killed by the hoverboard kitty!"
	Tag "Hoverboard Kitty"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		FETZ A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		FETZ BCDC 5 A_Chase
        Loop
	Missile:
		FETZ E 6 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget 
		FETZ F 4 A_CustomMissile("FetzyBarrel_Samsara", 32, 14)
		FETZ G 4 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
	Pain:
		OFFI F 5
		OFFI F 5 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		FETZ A -1
		Stop
    Raise:
		OFFI I 4
        OFFI H 4
        OFFI G 4
        OFFI F 4
        Goto See
	}
}

ACTOR BoomBarrel_Samsara replaces BoomBarrel
{
	Game Doom
	Health 5
	Radius 10
    Scale 0.80
    Height 56
	+SOLID
	+SHOOTABLE
	+NOBLOOD
	+ACTIVATEMCROSS
	+DONTGIB
	+NOICEDEATH
	+OLDRADIUSDMG
	DeathSound "world/barrelx"
	Obituary "$OB_BARREL"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		BARR A -1
		Loop
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetDamageType("Explosive")
	DeathContinue:
		TFOG A 4 BRIGHT A_Scream
		TFOG A 0 Radius_Quake(1,10,0,10,0)
        TFOG B 4 BRIGHT A_Explode
		TFOG C 4
		TFOG D 4
		TFOG EFG 4
		TFOG H 4 A_BarrelDestroy
		Stop
	Death.ZorchPistol:
	Death.Zorch:
	Death.ZorchKamikaze:
	Death.PhasingZorch:
	Death.ZorchSpectral:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetDamageType("Zorch")
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("BLOODLESSIMPACT",true)
		goto DeathContinue
	}
}
